About the author & Source Acknowledgements:

Madurakavi Srinivasa Ayyangar is the author of this work. He lived in a small village in
Madurai  district  during  the  early  part  of  twentieth  century.  (He  is  different  from
Madurakavi Azhwar (one of the twelve Azhwars). He is well known for the innumerable
poems composed by him. He had  left  the  manuscript  copy  of  this  work  with  Madurai
Tamil Sangam. It was printed and published by Thiru. R. Govindarajan, Chennai in 1990
with financial assistance provided by Govt. of India. We are grateful  to  him  for  having
accorded permission to publish it in Project Madurai. The  present  release  contains  only
the moolam of the work and does not include the notes and commentaries in the printed
book.
